Municipal Education Bureau Calls Principals for Talks 107

Shanghai South and Zhabei District Municipal School Principals

The Shanghai Special City Education Bureau has the custom of convening principals of various municipal and private schools for talks before the near end of the semester to report on past business, discuss future plans, and resolve emerging difficulties. The intention is very good. Now that the 18th year is about to end, Director Chen has again convened meetings in phases.

The Shanghai South District Municipal School Principals' Talk was held at the bureau at 2:00 PM on the 17th, with 27 people attending, as well as Secretary Ni and Section Chief Jiang from the Education Bureau. Director Chen chaired the meeting, and Yao Gengqing took the minutes. After the ceremony, the Director reported on: (1) the content of the plans for the implementation of compulsory education and the improvement of elementary school education from the All-Education Conference, as well as his own opinions on these plans; (2) the future direction of education in the city obtained from the All-Education Conference; (3) the hope that those serving in the education field as principals would not only focus on one school as their personal goal; (4) please ask the principals to work hard and tell the truth; (5) the attitude of this bureau towards recovering the educational rights in the concessions is that this work is actively seeking benefits for the citizens of the concessions, and it is not just passively cracking down on bad private schools; (6) the results of the elementary school curriculum standards experiment, hoping that the schools will report as soon as possible in order to gather and study them; (7) at the end of this semester, a city-wide graduation examination for elementary school students will be held to test the level of graduates from various elementary schools and to prepare for improving the level in the future, but it will not be judged solely on the basis of one day's performance; (8) schools should pay attention to the public display of students' usual grades to improve them; (9) active attention should be paid to Mandarin teaching; (10) teachers of natural sciences and social sciences should be well prepared and should not pretend to understand what they do not. After Director Chen finished speaking, the principals presented various questions and asked the Director to answer them. There were more than eighty questions regarding teaching, moral education, and equipment. The Director answered them one by one, and the meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

The Zhabei District Municipal School Principals' Talk was convened at the bureau at 2:00 PM on the 18th, with Director Chen, Secretary Ni, and the principals of the schools attending. Director Chen chaired the meeting, and Zhang Angqian took the minutes. After the ceremony, the Director reported on the experience of attending the National Education Conference: (1) implementing compulsory education; (2) training teachers; (3) teacher salaries; (4) collecting tuition fees; (5) foreigners running elementary education in China; (6) recovering educational rights in the concessions, and detailed the points that the municipal schools should improve, such as Mandarin teaching, teaching preparation, school hygiene, and sports fields. Then, the principals reported on the current situation of their respective schools. Finally, the Director gave a reply and the meeting adjourned, which was very satisfactory.

Ma Junwu Takes Office as Principal of Zhonggong School 110

Hu Shih's Resignation

Hu Shih, the principal of China Public School, once submitted his resignation last winter. However, due to a lack of a successor at the time, it was postponed until today when he formally submitted his resignation. After the board of directors approved it, Mr. Ma Junwu was invited to succeed him as the head of Zhonggong. Mr. Ma held an inauguration ceremony at the main hall of the school in Wusong on the 19th of this month. Chairman Cai Jiemin of the board of directors personally went to supervise the oath. The ceremony was held in accordance with etiquette. First, former Principal Hu delivered an opening speech, briefly stating that his resignation was not due to environmental pressure, as rumored by the outside world. If he was afraid of environmental pressure, he should have resolutely resigned last year and not waited until today. Mr. Ma was selected by us after a long period of searching. He is an old teacher of this school and a scientist with a great reputation in China. In the future, he will definitely bring unlimited glory to this school. Then, Mr. Cai delivered a speech, the general idea being that Mr. Hu and Mr. Ma have completely the same academic ability and moral integrity, and he cited various disciplines to prove this. Then, Mr. Ma Junwu delivered an inaugural speech, with many sincere appeals, hoping to share responsibility with the former principal and promote the glory of the school. Mr. Ma did not speak much because he was ill. Then, Gao Yihan delivered a speech, with four hopes: 1. To maintain the spirit of freedom of speech and express academic ideas. 2. To improve the material treatment of teachers so that they can teach with peace of mind. 3. To enrich the library to the minimum extent and become the most perfect library in Shanghai. 4. To increase the school's funding so that students can study for free in the future. Mr. Gao regarded these four hopes as what the school should do in order to reach the leading position of the highest institution of learning in the country. Finally, Yao Fangren, the representative of the student union, delivered a welcome speech, with three expectations for the new principal: (1) to quickly solve the school's registration problem; (2) to complete the new school building as soon as possible; (3) to continue and promote the spirit of former Principal Hu. After the ceremony, the Mathematics and Physics Department held a banquet for Mr. Ma, and the evening ended with joy.

Gao Shike Changed Name of Daxia University 112

In Accordance with Department Regulations, Changed to Teachers' Training Program

Daxia University added a Higher Normal Teachers' Training Program in the autumn of 1925, recruiting graduates from senior high schools and providing them with two years of higher normal education. The students who have graduated in the past have reached more than 200, and those who serve in educational administrative organs in various provinces and middle schools are well received. When the school was registered last year, the Ministry of Education recognized that the performance of the training program was excellent and allowed it to continue. However, it pointed out that the name "Higher Normal Department" was inconsistent with the newly promulgated academic system. The school affairs meeting decided that the name would be changed to Teachers' Training Program from the autumn to comply with the department regulations. As for the admission qualifications and length of study, they remain the same as before. The curriculum content after the autumn of this year has been planned by Dr. Huang Jingsi, director of the department, and has been greatly improved, making it more practical and applicable than before. The enrollment date will still be held at the same time as the various colleges of the school.

Grand South Bank Officially Opens Yesterday 115

Clearly Separating Finances to Become an Independent Commercial Institution

Hoping for Development to Assist Villagers of Zhenru

National Jinan University originally had a school bank, but due to its limited scope and entanglement with school finances, its business was difficult to develop. President Zheng recognized this early on and deemed it necessary to establish an independent bank. Preparatory personnel were then hired to actively plan, and after half a year, all matters were in order. A formal opening ceremony was held yesterday, presided over by economic expert Yang Ru , who reported that the bank was separated from the school's finances and was purely an independent commercial institution. Business procedures are entirely in accordance with ordinary banks. Because it is located at Jinan University, it is named Grand South Bank. The purpose is to facilitate the savings, loans, and remittances of all teachers and students, and to provide practical opportunities for students in the School of Business. However, it is different from banks attached to ordinary business schools, because this bank also undertakes entrusted businesses. Subsequently, Manager Ye Yuan reported on the preparations, the current deposits, and the hope that future business development would achieve: 1. Direct remittances and trade with overseas countries; 2. Helping villagers in the rural areas of Zhenru with business and production. Then, guest Zhang Tianfang delivered a speech as a neighbor of the Zhenru New Village workers and Jinan University. Mr. Hong Zhiling said that Grand South Bank has two relationships: one with bookworms, and two with wasteful people, mixing seriousness with humor. Afterwards, Manager Ye hosted tea and snacks at the cooperative, and the meeting adjourned. It is reported that the bank will soon apply to the government for registration to solidify its foundation.

A Laughing Matter · Hai · Ke 118

Guest: I heard that your house is famous for its antiques. Could you possibly allow me the pleasure of viewing them?

Servant: I'm very sorry. Our wife and young lady have both gone out. They two are the two most famous antiques.

Son: Father, I don't want to study arithmetic. It's been giving me headaches for the past few days.

Father: What are you talking about? When you grow up, if you don't know numbers, how will you be able to go to the gambling den and win people's money?

Villager: If you want to go to the village, you must follow this road.

Traveler: But don't you see the signpost by the side of the road? Doesn't it clearly indicate which road to take?

Villager: That is specially for tricking beggars, refugees, and bandits, so that they take the wrong road and don't get to the village.

A: Today I had something to say to you, but I'm very forgetful. I can't remember it for a moment.

B: Could it be something important?

A: Ah, I remember. "See you tomorrow."

A: I am very happy. Today my daughter is engaged to a young man. He is really a head above the rest.

B: That's right. I saw him yesterday. He is over six feet tall.

A Small Record of the Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Chen Ying Shi Martyr's Memorial Hall · Wu · Da · Sheng 119

Revolutionary martyr Mr. Chen Ying Shi has been dead for fourteen years. On the eighteenth of this month, the entire Lake Society held a groundbreaking ceremony for Martyr Chen at Shousheng Nunnery in front of Beijing Road. Many celebrities attended. Now, I will record the trivial details not mentioned in the newspapers to leave a fitting memorial.

A Commemorative Stool In the center of the ceremonial platform was a portrait of Sun Yat-sen. Below it was a photograph of Martyr Chen. In front was a rectangular stool. It is said that when Martyr Chen and his comrades attacked the Nanshi Arsenal that year, he was tied to this stool by Yuan Shikai's men and beaten with whips. However, the martyr felt that the physical pain was not important and did not diminish his revolutionary aspirations. Therefore, everyone still has a hundred percent respect for this commemorative stool.

Neatly Dressed Students The groundbreaking song that day was sung by students from middle and elementary schools in Huzhou who were living in Shanghai. The male students of the school wore gray uniforms, which were very solemn. The female students also wore dark blue cheongsams, which were very beautiful.

Mayor Zhang Personally Lays the Foundation That day, Mayor Zhang Qun personally laid the foundation. He held a hoe in both hands, moved the soil, and carefully placed the foundation stone. It was not until five minutes later that it was finished. Although Mayor Zhang was very strenuous at this time, he felt very comforted in his spirit.

Snippets from the Four University Speech Competition · San · Jiu 120

On the fourteenth of this month, the Jinan, Jiaotong, Guanghua, and Fudan Four University Mandarin Speech Competition opened at the Zhiyuan Hall of Jinan University. More than a thousand students from various schools attended, making it a grand occasion. Now, I will record the snippets of it, which readers will probably be happy to hear.

The Layout of the Venue The form of the venue was very similar to that of the Peking Grand Theater. On the left side of the stage was the seat for the four timekeepers sent by the four schools. On the right side was the seat for the eight speakers. In front of the timekeeper's seat was a square table about ten feet long. At first glance, it was no different from a temporary court courtroom.

The Romance of China and the West A certain actor spoke about the word "life" and extended it to the romance of China and the West. He said that Westerners' lives are quite orderly. They go from the lively period of childhood to the love period of middle age, from the love period of middle age to the fame and fortune period of adulthood, and finally to the leisure and enjoyment period of old age. Chinese people are all messed up. The reason is that China lacks a love period. Because China only has one "bedroom love" after marriage. Apart from the bedroom, there is simply no love to talk about. Although it is said that it has progressed now, it is another kind of so-called "tool love." The so-called tool love means that if a certain lady likes literature, I will use literature to try to date her. If a certain lady likes to watch movies, I will invite her to watch movies. I always want to use a tool to get her favor. This actor spoke with humor, and the audience burst into laughter.

The Victory of the Northwest A certain actor wanted to cater to the trend, so he talked about the novel topic of "Going to the Northwest." As a result, he actually won the championship.

Cotton Was Favored There was also a very strange topic called "Cotton." He said that cotton has a great relationship with the politics and economy of Sinology and should be promoted. As a result, he also got second place. After the verdict, everyone said that the judges favored cotton.

The Beauty Trap Failed A certain university selected a female representative to participate last year and actually won the championship trophy. This year, they used the same trick again, but unfortunately it failed. (But rewarded)

Climbing the First Pavilion in Songjiang · Qing · Song · Ju · Shi 121

Above the head gate of my Song County Office, there are several pavilions, square and tall, facing the thoroughfare in front, separated by a corridor in the middle, and facing the official residence in the back, which can be a place for the people of this county to visit. However, it has been in disrepair for many years and is about to collapse. Even if one wants to climb it, it is very dangerous, and it is often guarded by iron generals, so it is difficult to enter. Since County Magistrate Jin took office, all government affairs have been made public, and he wanted to repair it and use it as a place for officials and people to relax. At first, he had the ambition but did not achieve it. Last year, he collected money to build it beautifully and refurbished it, so that people could climb the steps, ascend, and indulge their ambitions. On the fifth day of the fifth month of this year, the sun was shining and the breeze was gentle, and I was flying with excitement. I walked slowly to the bottom of the pavilion. There are dozens of stone steps winding up, for tourists to go from the bottom to the top, directly to the pavilion. I climbed the steps to the middle floor, which is surrounded by stone railings on all sides, where one can look far and wide. In the center of the four walls, there are many stone inscriptions, which were inscribed by those who came to guard this county during the Ming and Qing dynasties. Unfortunately, I am forgetful and cannot remember them. I think they are just official articles, saying nice things. One more floor up, the windows are bright and the tables are clean, free from dust. Reading books and newspapers, the furnishings are elegant, no less than a public entertainment department for the people. This cannot but praise Mr. Jin for taking the people's hearts as his own and opening the door of convenience, and giving the people of Songjiang the joy of visiting. Turning forward again, the plaque stands tall, saying "The First Pavilion in Songjiang." The calligraphy is vigorous, thin, and hard, communicating with the gods. It is said that it was written by a famous Yuan person, but there is no need to delve into it. The name of this pavilion is named after its shape and can be seen at a glance. Leaning on the railing and looking into the distance, the scenery is clear at a glance. Like combs, the city's market streets. The two peaks facing each other are the Fangta and Xilin Pagodas inside and outside the city. The vermilion and black colors are dazzling and magnificent, the Provincial Girls' High School. The earth's horizon rises like steamed buns, the mounds in the suburbs. Winding like a rainbow and towering to the left and right are the battlements of the surrounding city walls. All shapes and colors are all visible in front of the pavilion. I regret not bringing a quick lens to capture this image. Otherwise, it would be a wonderful picture.

A Record of Appreciating Roses in Little Guanyuan · Qiong 122

The rose is a flower that has always been famous and precious. Throughout history, those who have seen and recited it, such as Minister Chen's poem, call it "the most romantic rose in the world." It can be said to be the highest praise. Others, such as Fan Da and the Su Shi brothers, have also written articles. Examining its names, it has titles such as "Evergreen" and "Slender Guest," as seen in Qunfang Pu. In Huajing's five grades and five lives, the rose is the flower envoy. Unfortunately, good species have been rarely seen recently, so there is nothing to do but feel regret. Yesterday, I went to Little Guanyuan in Hejiuzhai, Zhabei, with the auspicious man Foqing. I saw more than two hundred kinds of roses. Each kind has been given a good name by Shanghai scholars. One kind is green. When it blooms, each branch has two pistils side by side, which Fan Duanyuan titled "Double Emerald Birds." One kind is purple, with white stripes in the middle, which Chen Xiaodie titled "Purple Carpet Snow." One kind is pure white, which Chen Gangshu titled "Ice Wheel at the Bottom of the Water." One kind is pink, which Li Haoran titled "Jade Beauty's Spring Thoughts." One kind is vermilion, with white dots on the petals, which Sun Yusheng titled "Rouge with Snow Dots." One kind is pure crimson, like velvet floating up, which Yan Duhe titled "Crimson Clouds in the Sky." The above kinds, once they are named by celebrities, complement each other. There is also a kind that is golden yellow. The flowers are extremely beautiful and rare in the world. Zhou Shoujuan titled it "Yellow Silk Young Woman." I asked Foqing to take a picture of it and publish it above, so that those who love this flower can see it with their own eyes.

Supplement to the Pygmy People · Qing · Yao 123

Yesterday, I read an article by Junshuo in this column, "Doubts about the Record of Viewing the Pygmy People," and cited Zeng Jize's diary when he was an envoy to Europe as evidence, and doubted its fabrication and forced physical resemblance. I have seen a book called "Thousands of Wonders," I do not know where it was published in Shanghai. It is probably similar to the Guangfangyan Hall of the Manufacturing Bureau, but I cannot be sure. I have only seen one volume of the second volume, and I cannot get a glimpse of the whole picture. It also contains a short story about short people, which can be used by readers to smile. Therefore, I have specially recorded it and answered Junshuo.

The human body is like a pygmy, which is a disease. There is no such thing as a dwarf country in the world. Westerners have often gathered short people from various countries and written them down in books for reference. There was an Englishman named Hudson, who was born in the second year of Chongzhen in the Ming Dynasty and died in the thirty-second year of Kangxi. He was thirty years old and only one foot and three inches tall. In the sixth year of Qianlong, there was a short man in France named Xiaoer. He weighed only one catty when he was born and only ten catties when he was six years old. When he was fifteen years old, he was more than two feet tall and died at the age of twenty-three. There was a short man in the Netherlands, born in the fourth year of Guangxu. There were nine brothers and sisters, who were no different from ordinary people. Only the youngest daughter was only seven inches tall when she was in swaddling clothes. When she was five years old, she was one foot and two inches tall and weighed more than two catties. When she was seven years old, she was one foot and five inches tall and weighed seven catties. Putting her on the table, her father was next to her, and the two were compared, like Mount Tai to a hillock. (There is a picture in this book) However, this girl is exceptionally intelligent. In addition to speaking her native language, she is also fluent in English, French, and German. She traveled to various countries, and viewers often threw money at her, which led to great wealth. However, her body was weak and could hardly bear the weight of her clothes. Her spine was like a human, but her feet were weak. A certain doctor in Paris examined her pulse and found that it was as weak as Yan Shou. She only slept eight or nine hours a day and often showed joy, without any worries. If someone gave her something, she would accept it and thank them respectfully. Also, the French Learned Newspaper contained the name of a Russian, who was nineteen years old and weighed only five French pounds and was one foot and six inches tall.

In addition, most of what is recorded is based on science. Unlike Zixu's disregard for short people, who did not investigate the reason for their existence. It comes from nature and is not related to grinding or twisting. Then there is something credible. In ancient times, our country had a dwarf clan, which was three feet tall, but Wei Zhao said, "A different name for the southwestern barbarians." His statement is also not accurate. I wonder how heaven created them at the beginning.

On the Spring Sports Meeting of Minli Middle School · Yan · Jin 124

In this time of late spring and early summer, when the weather is clear, schools everywhere are holding sports meetings to promote physical education and wipe away the shame of being the "sick men of East Asia." Yan Jin has repeatedly visited and feels that sports talents have become more popular in recent years. He is truly happy about it. The other day (the sixteenth), the wind was gentle and the sun was warm, and there was no dust or sand. It was the date of the spring sports meeting of his alma mater, Minli Middle School. He invited more than ten friends, including Guo Qimeng, Zhang Keqin, Jin Jisheng, and Shimizu Sanlang, to visit together. He felt infinite emotion. The school has 1,500 students, and more than 488 of them participated in the sports meeting, accounting for almost one-third of the entire school. By this analogy, there should be one million athletes among the three million students in our country. Isn't that great? It is a pity that other schools are not as universal in sports as my alma mater. I will not discuss the merits of their achievements for the time being. The school authorities have worked hard to promote it and make it popular, and their intentions are very good. I will record this to inform other schools.

Letter to the Editor To Mr. Zhuzhu, Reading the manuscript of He Tianjian's "Tinglin Plundering Woman" on the fourteenth, I think it is a misunderstanding of hearsay. The so-called woman surnamed XX is the wife of Xia of Lixiang. She took her children with her and took advantage of the tomb sweeping to return to her mother's house in Ning. Unexpectedly, when the ship arrived at Zhangjing, she was plundered by Zhang Zhaohua's men, who were bandits from Haizhou, and extorted a large sum of money. Fortunately, she was rescued by the anti-bandit army in a boat in Yangcheng River, Jiangsu. Now the family has been reunited. The woman is already middle-aged and has many children. Not only is she a middle-aged woman, but she has no charm to speak of. The bandits also had no intention of comparing Sha Chili to Zhangtai Willow. Only the huge sum of money was difficult to raise for a while, so the time was slightly delayed. I am a close relative of the Xia family, and I know the truth of the matter in the inside. I have respectfully presented it to Mr. Chen, hoping that it will be published in the "Letter to the Editor" column, so that it can be corrected. I am eagerly looking forward to it. With best wishes, Your sincere, Gu Puren of Tinglin.

European Travel Correspondence (54) · Liu · Hai · Su

Matisse's Sixtieth Birthday (A) 125

LesSoixanteansdeHenriMatisse

It was the day after Matisse's sixtieth birthday that the Matisse masterpiece exhibition was held at the Paul Rosenberg Gallery at 99 Rue du Faubourg Saint-Honoré in Paris. The masterpieces of this master of "the enjoyment of life" are on display. Among them, the recent works of this genius are mixed with his early works. There are sketches and oil paintings, about sixty in total. It is really a noble and rare opportunity. After visiting several times in a row, I realized a new flavor in the paintings of this genius. I felt that this time I was close to the real feeling of Matisse's paintings. Because seeing a few of his works occasionally in museums or galleries on weekdays cannot show his flavor. To study a writer, one must look at him from all aspects and periods. Not only for Matisse, but for all masters. Before, when I was in Japan, I had seen various Matisse picture albums or colored reproductions. Naturally, I had a slight understanding of Matisse's outline. Although I admired him a hundred and twenty percent, I still couldn't feel how profound the real flavor was. Today, it is the sixtieth birthday of this first genius of Europe. I have directly tasted most of his masterpieces in detail. This is really the first happy event in my life. At the same time, what I personally felt is as follows. The expression of artistic works is the development of mankind. The expression of "the struggle for life" is a biological phenomenon that arises from the necessity of the inner spirit. I feel that the characteristic of modern creators is to affirm the personality of each person through the transmission of works. Therefore, psychology has seized the position of "conceptualism," emphasizing the emotions awakened in the individual's heart. Such paintings, no matter what method they use, are ten thousand times higher than paintings with religious or story themes or paintings that imitate the external appearance of nature. It transcends the immediacy and randomness and is based on the permanent absoluteness, that is, human emotions. I do not recognize the ridiculous and narrow principle that a painting has its own special world, its own special rules, and its own purpose. Art is just a moment in the life of the universe. I now trust my previous proposition to oppose "laws." If you penetrate the work of art with intuition and savor it with emotion, what I mean by "absolute eternity" is not the way, kind, or number of the world we represent, but the release of emotions. Regarding these words, I am not afraid of anyone's criticism or even abuse that I am resisting some kind of idealism or some kind of formalism. I always feel that I have to say this.

Gold Price Reaches a New Peak 127

528.5 Taels

Import of Silver Requires Passports Yesterday, the gold price rose again. The market's volatility made it hard to predict. The fluctuation between opening and closing amounted to 7 taels. The general trend was upward. Foreign exchange markets were tight in both official and unofficial trades. Banks had strong confidence. As aggressive buyers emerged and foreign exchange became hard to buy, the price temporarily surged to a new high of 528.5 taels. Heavy selling caused the price to drop by 4-5 taels. The price decreased as sellers rose, like Zhifengyong, Yongchengchang, and Chunyuanyong. At first, the market price was steady. With the National Government issuing orders for silver imports that require a passport, public sentiment became bleak. Traders sold enthusiastically, breaking 520 taels. Foreign exchange markets also weakened.

Opening High, Adding About Five Taels Since yesterday was Monday, there was no trade for big bills. The opening price for the July contract was 522 taels, an increase of 4.9 taels. When the banks lowered the discount rate by 0.125 for USD and 0.25 for JPY and raised the rate for JPY by 0.005, the price was 7.6 taels after 10 o'clock. At 3 o'clock, the price was 22 taels. A moment later, as retail investors bought, the price rose to 1.67 taels. After 3:30, news came that importers needed passports to import silver, which caused fear among traders. When the market went into a selling frenzy, the price sharply fell by 4 taels. Silk and Tea, Haining Cocoon Prices Step Higher 135

In the various cities and townships of Haining County, this year's new cocoon harvest is not as abundant as that of Hangzhou County, but the quality of the cocoons is quite good. This is because the weather this year has been abnormal, and farmers who raise improved varieties account for 70% of the total. Native breeds mostly disappeared during the major sleep stage. The impact of improved breeds is still slight, so the cocoon bodies are better. The cocoon market has been open for eight or nine days, and the initial cocoon price was only 55.6-60 yuan. This is because farmers, in view of the excellent quality of the new cocoons, insisted on selling at high prices. Otherwise, they would take them back to reel silk. Therefore, the cocoon merchants had no choice but to raise cocoon prices and compete to collect them. Cocoon prices rose step by step, with Chang'an seeing the highest increase. The improved variety cocoons opened at 80 yuan yesterday morning, while Haining and other places were only at 75-6 yuan. Each merchant has been collecting more goods in recent days, and large batches of dry cocoons are being transported to Shanghai in batches.

Dry Cocoons Waiting for Transport at Chang'an Station 136

New cocoons from Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Haining, and other places have all been put on the market. The cocoon merchants have been open for more than a week, and each merchant's collection volume is higher than last year's. They are baking them day and night in order to transport them to Shanghai in batches. According to investigations, since the new cocoons from Zhejiang and Hangzhou have been put on the market, only 500-600 bales of dry cocoons have been transported to Shanghai. Currently, cocoon bales are piled up like mountains in the Chang'an Station area. The Railway Bureau is in urgent need of transport due to a lack of locomotives. The Huitong Company, which is contracted to load cocoon bales, has now sent a letter to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureau, requesting them to find a way to allocate more freight cars for loading and transport.

New Atmosphere in the Yushan Tea Market 137

Plain Tea Picking and Manufacturing Completed...New Tea Opening Price 30 Yuan

High Village Tea Not Yet Open...Tea Firms Opening 30

Yushan in Guangxin Prefecture is an important tea-producing area in Jiangxi Province. There are many local merchants operating foreign tea estates. In the most prosperous years, there were 50-60 tea firms in the entire county. In recent years, due to the influence of banditry, foreign sales have not been smooth, and the number of tea firms has decreased day by day. Last year, there was almost no tea market to speak of. This year, Yushan County's tea production is very abundant. The plain tea in various mountain households was completed a month ago. High village tea developed later, with only tender buds showing, and has not yet reached harvesting. Recently, because the Communist bandits have been besieged by the garrison, they have fled to Dexing and Leping. Tea firms are taking the opportunity to rise up. There are more than a dozen tea firms in Zhangcun Street, the concentration of the tea market. There are more than 20 tea firms in Tongjiafang, Zhengjiafang, Miaodi, Yingpanshan, and Xiaoyushan in the Wubang area. Plain low village tea has been opened by local and foreign guilds, with prices ranging from 22 yuan to 34-5 yuan. Each picul of tea is subject to an additional 2 yuan bandit suppression fee. Transactions are very active. As of today, the amount handled by each firm and foreign guilds has reached a huge 10,000 piculs. Mountain households are now relieved and have proposed a high price. Each firm's first batch of new tea will be successively opened on the 5th and 6th of this month, rushing to make Zhenmei to transport to Shanghai. The market has suddenly presented a new atmosphere.

Qimen Black Tea Officially Opens 138

Yesterday, the foreign tea market in this port was quite lively. More than 4,000 boxes of new samples of black tea from Qimen, Fuliang, Jiande, Ningzhou, and other routes were displayed in various tea warehouses. British firms such as Jardine Matheson and Jinlong paid special attention to the high village Qimen tea. As a result of city-wide negotiations, Qimen tea opened at 125-190 taels, 40-50 taels higher than last year, an unprecedented high price. It is heard that there is still a price of more than 200 taels being negotiated. However, dealers showed little interest in middle and low village tea. Black tea seems to have a trend of raising high and suppressing low.

The Food River Down Rice Market Becoming More Quiet 139

Yesterday, fewer than ten boats came from the inland to Zhabei. Local sales remained sluggish. The white japonica market became more quiet. The high-quality goods were sold by customers, while ordinary medium-quality goods had to be cleverly handled. Few people were interested in the new japonica rice from the previous season. Therefore, prices gradually fluctuated slightly to the left and right. Transactions were deserted and the situation was sluggish. Thin rice entering the market still lacked appetite. All the long-standing and half-cut boats feared deterioration due to the hot weather and had to sell at a discount. Fortunately, this type of goods was extremely rare, and it failed to affect the high-quality goods. Yangdu Xian rice arriving was still not popular, and it was said that the river would soon be exhausted, so there was no standard for market prices. Large plates all reported stability, and variable yuan transactions weakened. Customer sales were sluggish, and shade yuan was scarce. Each yuan had no increase or decrease for the time being.

Few sources arrived in the Southern Shanghai River. In this street market, the digestion of white japonica rice from Xixi, Suzhou, and Tongxiang was only slightly moving in retail. The market situation yesterday had no rise or fall. Currently, due to the exhaustion of both storage and arrivals, it will remain stagnant for the time being. The special top-quality japonica rice is still opened at 20 yuan, closed on the left. The thin early rice from Southern Gang, Sijing, and Chonggu slightly softened in the market, but buyers intended to trim down, and sellers intended to shout up, so there was a mutual interference trend at the beginning of the morning. Then, due to slightly connected entries and exits, the large plate continued to flatten. The Yangdu and each sharp rice followed the trend of foreign rice, with all parties watching due to the scarcity of goods. The market transaction was extremely dull. Both white yuan arrivals and sales were scarce, and the market once again reported flat fatigue.

Futures Flour's Fearsome Surge 140

Bulls Continue to Push High...Surge by Two Fen

Producers Dump Distant-Term...Follow the Rise Separately

Yesterday, the flour market once again showed a surge. The total daily transaction also reached about 700,000, with the bulls' chips exceeding all the existing flour owned by the producers. Therefore, they were squeezing the shorts at will. The five-and-a-half qian mark was no longer feared. It has already been reached, and the intention to raise it has not weakened. Therefore, in the morning, it was only slightly more than 0.05 yuan. By the afternoon, due to the short covering and more competition, the market surged again, with the highest price reaching 2.57 taels. However, it is speculated that the bullish speculation will not end until it has been raised to 2.6 taels. For distant-term months, because inland gangs were aware of the producer's dumping, this month has gradually risen extraordinarily, and the buying interest has been exceptionally strong. Among the gangs, the Xixi Gang was the most enthusiastic. Observing the subsequent steps, there is still a continued rise trend. As a result, May and June rose by 0.02 yuan compared to the previous day, July rose by 0.015 yuan, August and September each rose by 0.01 yuan, and October rose by 0.0075 yuan.

Futures Wheat Traded 200 Carloads 141

Although yesterday's wheat surge was not huge, the transaction volume for each month also reached about 200 carloads. With the current bullish and bearish forces, the strength is great. The bulls believe that the flour market is good, and the buying interest is naturally brave and unspeakable. The sellers believe that the weather is very good, and the harvest of new wheat in each producing area is expected to be better than in previous years. Therefore, they are also doing their best to sell. However, the current position of the bulls seems to be superior. Therefore, in the midst of the volatility of each month, it ultimately appeared good. As a result, June, July, August, and September each improved by 0.01 yuan compared to the previous week, and October improved by 0.03 yuan. Spot wheat is firm in standard steps, and the factory's appetite has not eased. However, the quoted price for high-car wheat has risen by another 0.02-0.03 yuan. The medium-quality has also brought up a lot. Kaixuzhou Nansuzhou Qingjiangpu Wheat is 5.15 taels, Hankou Wheat is 4.62 taels, for a total of 2,000 bags.

Jiangsu Province 146

Abolishing Harsh and Trivial Taxes

Provincial Government's Reply to the Chamber of Commerce and Industry Association

The Jiangsu Provincial Government replied to the Chamber of Commerce and Industry Association yesterday, stating: "In response to your letter, we have received your request from the Shanghai Special City Chamber of Commerce and Industry Association to reduce harsh and trivial taxes, and have instructed the department to verify and respond accordingly. The abolition of harsh and trivial taxes is enshrined in the party program and has been resolved and strictly implemented by former Director Zhang, and orders have been issued for compliance. Since taking office, the Director has handled all financial and administrative matters in accordance with the orders of the government. Recently, various counties have requested the collection of various donations for handling local undertakings. After careful consideration, weighing the urgency and importance, reductions and rejections have been made separately, and proposals have been submitted for deliberation, with the aim of benefiting the public without harming the people. For example, in Yangzhou, Dongtai, and other counties, the original donations for ships and cotton have been abolished separately, either because they conflict with the case or because they involve troublesome matters. In addition, any trivial new taxes that affect the livelihoods of the poor will be strictly rejected at any time to alleviate the people's difficulties. Therefore, we hereby submit this document in response."

Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement 148

The Truth About the Signing Process

According to the Guowen News Agency, the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement has been approved and implemented by the National Government. A dispute arose before its implementation, and outsiders are unaware of the true situation regarding this rapid change. Therefore, our agency's reporter specially inquired about the details of the process from Mr. So-and-so, an important figure in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs close to Minister Wang. The following is a record of the conversation to clarify the truth. The following is the reporter's questions and Mr. So-and-so's answers:

(Question) What exactly was the situation regarding the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' inadequate procedures in signing the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement this time?

(Answer) Minister Wang is an experienced diplomat and has always been extremely cautious. He has already signed new treaties with sixteen or seventeen countries in the past two years. He certainly knows the procedures. The reason for the controversy this time is simply because the agreement was announced too quickly. The agreement was signed at noon on the 6th of this month, and it was reported in the newspapers on the 7th. The official documents from the Ministry to the Executive Yuan had not yet arrived, but outsiders had already read it in full. As a result, members of the Legislative Yuan, after seeing the report, immediately raised concerns that the diplomatic authorities had exceeded their authority regarding the effectiveness of Article 5. Minister Wang went to Shanghai on official business after signing, and the Legislative Yuan held a meeting on the 10th, so he could not immediately explain the situation, which led to further doubts due to repeated rumors. In fact, Article 5 is one of the articles in the entire agreement, and all articles must be submitted to the National Government for approval before they can take effect. If the National Government does not approve it, then the effectiveness of the 10th is like the skin without the fur, where can the fur attach? In short, if the agreement had been announced after approval by the National Government, there would have been no misunderstanding this time.

(Question) Before the official signing, was the content of the agreement submitted to the government and the Yuan for discussion?

(Answer) The full text of the agreement and its attachments were approved by the Foreign Affairs Group of the Central Political Conference before signing. At the meeting on the morning of March 19, the Foreign Affairs Group members, such as the three Yuan Presidents Tan, Hu, and Wang, and the four Ministers Sun, Kong, Song, and Wang, were all present. At that time, Committee Member Wang, in his capacity as Minister, presented the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement and its attachments, which he had drafted with Japanese Ambassador Shigemitsu. After the members reviewed them, they considered them suitable for signing. President Wang Liangchou even personally wrote the words "Attachment One," "Attachment Two," and "Attachment Three" on the drafted agreement in pencil to indicate that the fourth attachment would not need to be included in the commercial treaty in the future. Minister Wang immediately stated that he would comply. This is an undeniable fact. However, as usual, the main articles of the treaty are the most important. The readers discussed the articles in Articles One, Two, and Three in detail, and only glanced at Articles Four and Five.

(Question) It is said that the provision on the effectiveness of Article 5 of the agreement was proposed by Minister Wang. What is its purpose?

(Answer) It was indeed Minister Wang's intention. Because Japanese diplomacy is very cunning, he feared that the signing would be delayed again and would not be implemented for a long time. Now, by setting a deadline for effectiveness, he hoped to quickly recover the Dalian and Andong Customs and implement the new tax rates, which could increase revenue by 300,000 to 400,000 yuan per month. Recently, with the soaring price of gold, international exchange rates have caused huge losses in the blink of an eye. The government wants the customs to be able to change the gold unit exchange rate according to the market price at any time to implement the autonomy of the exchange rate and recover the losses. Moreover, the new treaty on tariff autonomy has already been signed with various countries. Now, only Japan is obstructing it, giving other countries an excuse. This is a major obstacle to the promotion of tariff sovereignty. Therefore, he earnestly hopes that the Sino-Japanese Agreement will be implemented as soon as possible so that China's tariff autonomy can be promoted as a whole as soon as possible. He also believes that the government and the Yuan have long understood this intention and will definitely approve it without doubt.

(Question) Is China actually at a disadvantage in the provision for reciprocity?

(Answer) This time it is not reciprocity. According to the reciprocity method, both sides should reduce one-third or one-quarter of the current tax rates. However, according to Attachment One, not only will Japanese goods imported into China not be reduced, but some types can be increased by another 2.5%. However, it is stated that they will not be increased again within one or three years. As for cotton yarn, our country can levy a special tax again. Furthermore, regarding our country's goods exported to Japan, Japan also stated that the current tax rates will not be increased within one or three years, and the tax on silk and other items will be reduced by one-third. Therefore, on the surface, it seems that our country has the advantage and Japan is at a disadvantage. But in reality, it is not the case. Everyone knows that China's industry and commerce are not as good as Japan's. Most of our products are raw materials, and Japan does not levy taxes on them. It is impossible to make the types or values of goods reach a level playing field, just like placing a fat person and a thin person on opposite ends of a scale and trying to achieve a level balance. However, our side still achieves a level balance in the impossible, which is why our side levies a special tax on cotton yarn and adds another 2.5% to other types, while Japan reduces the tax on silk by one-third and does not add to other types. China can never permanently avoid signing a treaty with Japan, nor can it forcibly levy high tariffs on Japanese imports by force or order. Therefore, in order to gain diplomatic convenience and promote the entire tariff sovereignty, China can only make slight concessions. This is a matter of fact. For example, in a race, you can only strive forward; there is no reason to make people go backward, and this is the spirit of seeking mutual equality.

(Question) How about the provision in the attachment that 5 million yuan will be allocated annually for the purpose of reorganizing foreign debts?

(Answer) This provision was made by our country on its own initiative. In January of the 18th year of the Republic of China, the National Government instructed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to inform all relevant countries that our country would allocate 5 million yuan annually from customs duties to reorganize domestic and foreign debts, starting from that year. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs notified nine countries, including the United Kingdom, the United States, France, and Italy. This time, it is the same statement to Japan. It is also listed as a suspected use in the financial report of Minister Song at the Third National Congress. However, all of this naturally refers to legitimate domestic and foreign debts. In the future, when reorganizing with Japanese creditors, the scope should still be limited to legitimate debts.

(Question) Regarding the Legislative Yuan's review opinion, requesting a reprimand of the responsible authorities, it seems to blame the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

(Answer) Minister Wang never cares about the rights and wrongs of things at any particular time. As for reprimanding the responsible authorities, it is to pay attention to the organizational law of the National Government when concluding foreign treaties in the future. This is to warn against future problems and prevent them before they happen. Not only should the National Government issue this reprimand, but it is also what Minister Wang wants to request the National Government to issue a circular to reprimand.

Meeting of the Rice and Grain Price Stabilization Committee 155

Decided on the Selling Price of Rice and Grain

Passed the Detailed Rules for Operation

The Shanghai Special Municipality Rice and Grain Price Stabilization Committee held its third meeting at the Social Affairs Bureau at 1 p.m. on May 8. The committee members present were Yan Xiaoquan, Xu Fu (representing Xu Yang), Mo Zijing, Yuan Liang (representing Zhao Zhijia), Fan Hesheng, Zhu Zixiang, Sun Yishan, Weng Yinchu, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yiting, and Lu Wenshao. Chairman Pan Gongzhan presided over the meeting. The matters discussed were: (1) The procedures fees of the procurement group of this committee and the budget for the expenditures of the distribution group and the distribution points. It was resolved that: (1) The items in the budget are relatively close, but all expenses should be handled with absolute frugality. (2) This budget can be used as a reference when raising donations. (2) A resolution was passed regarding the decision on the selling price of stabilized rice. It was resolved that the foreign rice imported by this committee should be priced according to the recent market price of rice shops, which is about 15 yuan to 15.5 yuan per dan. However, rice shops have room for maneuver in terms of jin, liang, sheng, and he, so the selling price of this committee should be 5 jiao lower than the lowest market price. Therefore, it was unanimously passed to tentatively set the price of rice at 14.5 yuan per dan, based on 200 pounds per dan. (3) The draft of the detailed rules for operation of this committee was resolved and passed with amendments. (4) Omitted. (5) How to transport rice for sale in rural areas was resolved that the municipal committee members in each district should prepare the price and submit it to the Price Stabilization Committee. The quantity should be reported by each committee member to the Social Affairs Bureau for further verification. (6) The locations of the first and second distribution points are too close, and one of them should be temporarily suspended (temporary motion by Zhu Zixiang). It was resolved that the second point should be decided after considering the situation. If there is no need, it should be temporarily suspended. (7) How should this committee continue to urge donations? (Temporary motion by the chairman) It was resolved that the economic group should convene a meeting to decide. (8) The date of the next regular meeting was decided that the chairman should convene it on an ad hoc basis.

May 20th, 9th Year of the Republic of China (Shen Bao, Fourth Edition) Tuesday (14)

The Sanitation Campaign in this City 158

A Brief Explanation of Spitting and Hygiene

The news of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's hosting of the 5th Sanitation Campaign has been recorded in previous newspapers. It is heard that the bureau dispatched administrators and health inspectors to post slogans, distribute various printed materials, and supervise the street cleaners to clean up the work, which was very busy. Moreover, the bureau paid special attention to publicizing the work of preventing cholera this time. Among the slogans posted in various places, there were also many of this item. In addition, the bureau recently received a kind of brief explanation of spitting and hygiene issued by the Ministry of Health, which details the harm of spitting at will. The bureau has distributed it to citizens for attention in the past two days. There are many people in our society who commit the bad habit of spitting at will. The following is the original text of a brief explanation of spitting and hygiene in order to reform those who commit this bad habit.

Spitting and Hygiene Tuberculosis is caused by tuberculosis bacteria. Bacteria are microorganisms, a kind of very small living thing that cannot be seen with the naked eye. If we magnify them with a special magnifier called a microscope, we can see them. If there is no tuberculosis bacteria, tuberculosis will never occur. The range of tuberculosis bacteria spread is very wide, so many people are often unknowingly infected with tuberculosis because of contact with this dangerous object. However, although tuberculosis bacteria are widely present, their concentration and toxicity vary greatly from place to place. Like those scattered in the air, they are usually very thin and their toxicity is very weak. Conversely, the sputum of tuberculosis patients, their sputum foam is the most concentrated and has a strong toxic danger. If we use numbers and words to express their intensity, the air is equivalent to one, and the sputum is equivalent to one hundred million to one hundred billion. It can be seen that the sputum spread of the virus is terrible. The place where tuberculosis bacteria multiply is in the patient's diseased part. Although there are countless tuberculosis bacteria hidden in the body, when the lung disease is in its early stage, it is not mixed in the sputum and discharged from the body. The sputum foam in the transmission is not at all dangerous. After a certain period of time, the tuberculosis bacteria in the sputum will be mixed in the spit blood and discharged to the outside of the body, or the patient will swallow the sputum and mix it in the feces, and a large amount is discharged, or the patient himself suffers from intestinal tuberculosis, and it is discharged from the feces. Or like kidney tuberculosis, bladder tuberculosis, the patient's certain period can also discharge a large amount of tuberculosis bacteria from the urine, which is all contagious dangerous. In addition, nasal mucus, eye secretions, pus, milk, blood, etc. are also the causes of tuberculosis infection. All these sources of tuberculosis bacteria discharge should not be taken lightly and ignored. Among them, the most important thing in tuberculosis prevention is sputum. Now let's divide sputum into four types according to the degree of danger. The first is the sputum spit out by the patient, including the sputum in the sputum bowl and the cloth or paper with viscous sputum. The second is the sputum foam spit out by the patient's cough and sneeze, including the sputum foam when talking and laughing. The third is the general articles, food and drink, and fingers attached to the patient's sputum or sputum foam. The fourth is the air scattered in the dust after the sputum or sputum foam dries. In terms of these four types, the size of its danger is the same as their order. Spitting is very important. Tuberculosis bacteria are colorless microorganisms. Assuming that we make them red, then the sputum will be very thick red. As for the items around the patient's bedding, they can also be regarded as dots of red. The fingers of the caregiver can also be dyed the color of red sputum. The sputum color is thick, which means important. The sputum has a strong adhesion, and sputum foam is easily attached to objects, and can stay anytime and anywhere. Although it dries and peels off later, it is difficult to reduce the danger, but it can preserve it for a long time. The resistance to drying is very strong. After several months, and even years, it still does not lose its vitality and infectivity. This dried sputum is gradually ground into powder and scattered in the air with the dust, or with the fine silk of clothes, paper, cloth, etc., and then invades people's respiratory organs. Also, flies are very good at licking sputum, or sticking sputum on their feet, and then they fly to people's mouths or food, or fly to the neighbor's house, reaching far away, and it is easy to spread tuberculosis bacteria anytime and anywhere, so the most dangerous thing to be infected is sputum. However, there is a big difference in the intensity of tuberculosis infection between new sputum and dry sputum. Directly inhaling the sputum foam from the patient's cough and sneeze is new sputum, which is very dangerous and has a strong infection. If you inhale air with very thin dry tuberculosis bacteria, this is dry sputum, which is less dangerous and has a weak infection. In the middle of these two, there are also various levels. It can be seen that it is not good to spit at will anytime and anywhere, and it can infect people regardless of the size of the danger. Tuberculosis bacteria invade the body and do not directly cause disease. If it reaches the lungs, it becomes pulmonary tuberculosis, and it does not directly cause disease. It takes several months to decades to gradually spread. However, tuberculosis bacteria are not limited to always proceeding so slowly. If you get a suitable opportunity to invade and facilitate proliferation, it can also proceed rapidly. So the onset of tuberculosis is after infection, as early as dozens of days, and as late as decades, and the symptoms of onset are very clear, and there are also completely unclear. A pulmonary tuberculosis patient can cough up tens of millions of tuberculosis bacteria in 24 hours. When the patient coughs heavily, fine sputum foam is often sprayed out of the mouth. All people within three or four feet can be harmed by it. If this sputum foam does not directly invade people, it will fall on the ground and soon dry out with dust, spreading in the phlegm-containing mucus. When it dries, it sticks firmly, and it is not easy to wash off, and it becomes a contagious preparation object. All sputum spat on the ground or in trams, trains, and public places is very harmful to people. Sometimes our soles or skirt hems, if they stick to undried sputum, and living bacteria can lead the bacteria into our homes, and gradually become dust. If it is in a place with insufficient sunlight, the life of the bacteria will live longer, and our lives will suffer more infectious disasters, because the bacteria cannot move automatically in the dark, but brooms and feather dusters can help them fly and scatter on household items. Whoever uses these items has the risk of inhaling bacteria and the opportunity to infect tuberculosis, so never spit anytime and anywhere to avoid the spread of this bacteria. Sputum should always be spit in a sputum bucket or sputum bowl, etc. If you want to prevent flies from flying around the sputum bowl, you can add a lid, and you can add water to the sputum bucket. It would be better if you could add disinfectant and antiseptic solution to the sputum bucket, such as the above. If you have a fairly large clean paper, or new cotton gauze or cloth, etc., when you can't find a sputum bucket or sputum bowl for a while, spit on them and then burn them, that's even better. Also, when coughing and sneezing, whether it is yourself or others, you should use this paper or cotton gauze or cloth or small handkerchief, etc., to cover your mouth and nose, and you can also prevent the spread of sputum foam if you have to use your hands. Be careful when talking to tuberculosis patients. This paper, cotton gauze, cloth, etc., should also be disinfected in the same way. Do not spit at will anywhere, whether it is in a house, on land, or on the floor. Everyone should do this, always do this, and be careful to encourage each other to prevent and reduce the occurrence of tuberculosis. In addition, do not swallow tuberculosis to avoid damaging appetite, causing intestinal tuberculosis, and allowing tuberculosis bacteria to exist in feces, discharge and spread. The sputum bucket, sputum bowl, etc. used should also be disinfected at any time. The best disinfection method is steaming and boiling. If it is not easy to do, a simple method is to repeatedly rinse with boiling water and expose it to the sun more.

Health Bureau Will 159

Give Cholera Vaccinations to Workers

The Shanghai Special Municipality Health Bureau sent a letter to various factories, stating: "Respectfully informing you that cholera (commonly known as 'luo sha jiao chang sha' or 'diao jiao sha') frequently occurs in Shanghai every summer and autumn, causing great harm. Based on the bureau's investigations over the years, laborers are particularly susceptible to cholera. This is because laborers' living conditions are simpler, and they often only seek cheap food and drink without careful selection, which is one reason why laborers are prone to cholera. Secondly, laborers work in crowded places with frequent contact, so if one person has cholera, it is easily spread. Workers are the most important element of a factory's production. From the perspectives of moral sentiment, industrial economics, and long-term planning, factories should relieve workers of this unknown suffering. This aligns with the virtues of universal love and mutual assistance, and it is also the key to harmonious collective work. This bureau has submitted a proposal to the Shanghai Special Municipal Government, which has been approved, to promote cholera vaccinations this year, especially focusing on laborers and those living in shantytowns. The bureau will schedule personnel to administer the vaccinations, all free of charge, without any expense to the factories. However, regarding the laborers, their education levels vary, and they may not fully understand these preventative measures, or they may be stubborn, viewing epidemics as natural disasters and believing they are unavoidable, or they may start but not finish due to slight reactions from the vaccination (each person must be vaccinated twice to be effective). In order to prevent epidemics, protect laborers, maintain social economy, and increase productive capacity, this bureau will schedule personnel to your factory to administer cholera vaccinations. It is hoped that your manager, along with staff and foremen, will first enthusiastically educate the workers, so that everyone receives the vaccination to prevent epidemics and value life. Attached is a simplified Chinese notice. Please review it and explain it to the workers to enlighten them and put it into practice. Also, please fill out and return the enclosed application form so that we can schedule personnel to administer the vaccination at your factory."

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau 160

Requests Instructions on Relief Measures for the Cotton Textile Industry

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau believes that the cotton textile industry in this city is declining daily and urgently needs relief. Having no ideas, they specifically submitted a request to the Municipal Government yesterday for instructions. The original request is transcribed in full below: "Submitting a request for instructions: It has been observed that recently, over a dozen cotton textile factories in this city have successively closed down. The remaining factories are mostly in precarious situations and may close at any moment. The factory owners in this industry have repeatedly appealed for a reduction in wages to ease the burden so that they can勉力搘撑. However, the workers in this industry claim that their wages are already low and request that the conditions be revised and wages increased to maintain their livelihood. After investigating the logic and emotions on both sides, the bureau feels that neither can be faulted. The bureau feels particularly challenged in resolving this situation. The cotton textile industry has been deeply affected by the economic invasion of foreign merchants, making it difficult to compete with them. In addition, heavy taxes, slow sales, accumulation of inventory, and difficulties in financial turnover have led to repeated bankruptcies and closures. The request to reduce wages cannot be approved because it is not convenient. However, if expenses are not reduced and costs lowered, there will inevitably be a day when it is impossible to continue. Moreover, in the current situation of 米珠薪桂, the difficult living conditions of cotton textile workers are also a reality. However, if a wage increase is approved, it would be equivalent to accelerating the demise of the cotton textile industry. 皮之不存, 毛將焉傅 The bureau believes that the fundamental solution still lies in alleviating all the current difficulties of the cotton textile industry, such as how to circulate accumulated goods, how to provide financial assistance, and how to reduce taxes. All of this seems beyond the capabilities of a single city. The bureau is troubled and unable to make a decision. Furthermore, recalling the past winter when the industry requested relief funds, efforts were repeatedly made to coordinate with the National Goods Bank and others, but all were ineffective. The direction of handling is unknown. Therefore, this document is prepared and submitted, requesting that your Excellency review it and issue instructions for compliance. This is for the public good. Respectfully submitted to Mayor Zhang."

The Lake Society held its sixth members' general meeting at the Huzhou Alumni Primary and Secondary School Girls' Department in Zhengxiu Lane, Kaifeng Road, on the morning of the 18th of this month. Ling Songru, representative of the Fundraising Committee for the Construction of the Society's Headquarters, reported on the third fundraising effort. After a break for lunch, at 2:00 PM, a groundbreaking ceremony for the Yingzhi Memorial Hall, the new headquarters of the society, was held at the address of the new headquarters at the corner of Beijing Road and Guizhou Road. In addition to the members, over two hundred guests attended. The Public Security Bureau Military Band played music to open the meeting. Chairman Chen Aishi reported on the Lake Society's purpose in establishing the Yingzhi Hall. The Mayor of Shanghai Special Municipality laid the foundation stone. The junior central department students of the Huzhou Alumni Primary and Secondary School in Shanghai sang a groundbreaking song. Ye Huijun and others gave speeches. At 3:30 PM, photos were taken again at the meeting venue on Kaifeng Road. (2) Recover the site of the former Huzhou Prefecture Office. (3) Urge the government to establish Yingzhi Sericulture School. (4) Request the Zhejiang Provincial Government to allocate more disaster relief funds and organize a disaster relief association to save the disaster victims in Huzhou. (5) Request the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui to thoroughly plan the suppression of bandits to save the lives of the people. (6) Plan the construction of the Huzhou Alumni Primary and Secondary School building in Shanghai. (7) Request the Zhejiang Provincial Government to protect cocoon merchants, etc. Next, Pan Gongzhan, Chen Aishi, Zhou Youqian, Chen Guofu, Zhou Yueran, Chen Lifu, Shen Yanxiang, Shen Jiesheng, Shen Tianxin, Qian Xinzhi, Wang Yiting, Yao Yinfo, Ling Songru, Tang Jicang, Yang Pusheng, Qiu Peihao, Tang Boqi, Niu Shiyu, Zhou Peizhen, Li Boqin, and Lu Si'an were elected as the twenty-one executive committee members. Zhang Jingjiang, Dai Jitao, Zhu Liuxian, Yan Junyi, Yu Huancheng, and others were elected as the five supervisory committee members. The meeting concluded with tea and refreshments.

Jisheng Society Held Relief Meeting Yesterday 162

The Chinese Jisheng Society held a relief meeting in this city yesterday. The chairman and vice-chairmen Wang Yiting, Xu Qianlin, and Huang Hanzhi, as well as over thirty committee members, attended. First, Chairman Wang announced the purpose of the meeting and requested the two directors of relief economics to report on recent situations. Although winter relief was provided last year, it was just a drop in the bucket. Next, the Economics Director reported that our association has received considerable assistance and donations from comrades and enthusiastic people from all walks of life. There are even women who have sold their ornaments to help the relief effort. The disaster victims are fortunate to receive such kind assistance, but the disaster is widespread, and universal relief is difficult. According to the current report from the Relief Director, only one-thousandth of the national disaster area is receiving relief. The current budget of our association is severely short. Please collect the advance funds that you all have agreed to pay, etc. Chairman Wang said, "Our association is an organization formed by compassionate comrades who have come together. We are fulfilling our relief duties with conscience. We will do as much relief work as we can with our capabilities. We hope everyone will work hard and never give up to achieve our goal." It is highly possible that things will be stranded one day.' After careful consideration, this is indeed the truth. It is hoped that you will jointly devise good strategies and recruit compassionate and benevolent people from all over the world to participate as much as possible in order to maintain long-term operations." Chairman Wang deeply agreed with his words, and the majority unanimously agreed, hoping that someone with human and financial resources can do whatever they can, save whoever they can, and rely on their conscience to invoke heavenly harmony and reverse the浩刧. There is probably a chance to get something done.

The Chamber of Commerce Union Begins Reorganization 163

The Printing Press Union of the Commercial Press on Baoshan Road, Zhabei, in this city has been established for many years. It has a large membership and occupies a significant position among various unions. Recently, due to the complexity of internal elements and frequent disputes, the People's Training Committee of the Municipal Party Department has repeatedly received requests for sanctions from many union members. The eighth meeting resolved to reorganize the union. The rationale is recorded below:

The Reasons for the Citizen Training Committee to Reorganize the Chamber of Commerce Union: The committee previously received a joint accusation from workers such as Zhang Youquan of the Chinese character department of the Commercial Press Printing Press, alleging that the executive supervisory committee of the union colluded with the Communist Party, conspired to revolt, and asked that they be punished quickly to stop the trouble. While this was being reviewed, another statement from Xing Aiqing and other workers from the lead printing department listed facts, accusing the executive supervisory committee of inciting labor unrest, being hostile to the government, harboring reactionaries, and plotting illegal activities, and requested a prompt investigation. Furthermore, Shi Jinguan and other workers from the binding department submitted a request stating that the union was being run by the wrong people, the workers were repeatedly oppressed, reactionaries were rampant, and the environment was dangerous, and they appealed for severe punishment of the leaders and reorganization of the union. After investigation, it was found that the Chamber of Commerce Printing Press Union has been run by the wrong people in recent years. Internal disputes have repeatedly arisen, the organization is loose, the elements are complex, the corrupt are taking the opportunity to collect money and exploit the workers, and the unscrupulous are taking the opportunity to incite and disrupt the public order. They even despise the government and violate party orders, with numerous flaws and obvious crimes. One or two examples are listed below to summarize the rest. It was found that before the party convened the Third National Congress, the Central Committee ordered all levels of people's organizations to suspend meetings during the meeting period. However, union committee members Tan Huanxiang, Ge Hecai and others disregarded the law and arbitrarily convened secret meetings of various unions on March 12, plotting to oppose the Third Plenary Session and pushed representative Gu to go to Beijing to participate in the National People's Congress called by the reactionaries to confront the Third Plenary Session of the Party. The evidence was established, and the Sixth District Party Department impeached them. Later, the party headquarters gave them a light warning, but on June 8 of the same year, the union secretly convened a meeting of various unions in Zhabei, with Communist Party remnants such as Zhou Feng participating in it, plotting an uprising. Fortunately, the party headquarters noticed it and went with the Public Security Bureau to stop it, and no incident occurred. Therefore, the Sixth District Party Department decided at the Third Plenary Session to expel Tan Huanxiang and Ge Hecai from the party to warn the others. However, the party headquarters was broad-minded and only warned Tan et al., hoping that they would turn over a new leaf. However, the union thought that the party headquarters did not dare to compete with it, so it intensified its efforts to expel a large number of comrades in retaliation. When the association went to negotiate, they threatened to strike. On the one hand, they resumed the excessive collection of special donations, and engaged in private corruption. Later, after the workers reported the matter, the Social Affairs Bureau intended to inspect its accounts, but the union refused to hand them over and dared to incite other unions to unanimously oppose the government's audit. As a result, the Nanhuo Industry Workers' Union and others followed suit. Recently, the union went on strike without authorization because it was not able to obtain a wage increase, and it demanded rice subsidies without mediation. Its actions of shaking people's hearts and disrupting the rear were very obvious. The Central Committee had already stipulated that there would be no holiday for the May 9th Memorial, but the union argued strongly and dared to stop work without authorization. Its contempt for the law and its hostility to the government are largely similar. This committee deeply believes that tolerance will only breed evil, and forbearance will only prolong chaos. A single spark can start a prairie fire, and a trickle will turn into a river. If the Chamber of Commerce Printing Press Union disregards laws, is hostile to the government, colludes with reactionaries, and plots illegal activities, if it is not resolved early, the consequences will be endless. Therefore, the committee decided at its eighth meeting to order the Chamber of Commerce Printing Press Union to suspend its activities and await reorganization. The current executive supervisory committee members of the union should be dismissed, and Wang Wenhua and other seventeen people should be appointed as reorganizers, and Hou Dachun and Yang Qingyuan should be appointed as instructors. In addition to sending orders and letters separately, the reasons for reorganizing the union are briefly stated on the right for your information. The People's Training Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

Yawo Sand 166

Pirates Kidnap People for Ransom

Five Men and Women Kidnapped Successively

Three People Demanded 15,000 Yuan in Ransom

Meeting Arranged at Crescent Moon Harbor

To Redeem from Master Shen San

In the Yawo Sand area, located about a dozen miles offshore from the Wusong estuary, piracy has been rampant recently, and major kidnapping cases have occurred from time to time. A certain person with the surname of Mou was kidnapped from the sand some time ago and was redeemed for 1,000 yuan. The person had just been released when, at about 9:00 PM the other night, Ma Baoshan, the third small owner of the Mahetai Fish Shop in Dongzhen, aged 26, was having dinner at home with his wife and three-year-old daughter when suddenly many pirates came, each armed with pistols and Mauser guns, and tied up Ma and his wife and daughter and took them to the bandit ship. The bandits then went to Xizhen, when it was already 10:00 PM, intending to kidnap the owner of Gu Hengmao Grocery Store, but the owner was not there, so they kidnapped his concubine and two shop assistants. It has been over a week now, and although the families of the two have been searching everywhere, there has been no news. Until yesterday, the Ma family received a letter from the bandits, saying that they needed to prepare 15,000 yuan and go to Master Shen San's place at Crescent Moon Harbor near Caozhen to redeem the three Baoshan couples, etc. After receiving the letter, Ma Xingfan, Baoshan's father, was very anxious because the other party was asking for too much money and he could not afford it. The person is an ordinary businessman and not from a wealthy family. Recently, there has been a large population and difficult living conditions, resulting in income not meeting expenses, so he has no ability to rescue his sons, etc.
